## 1 abase 降低（地位、声望等）  

Degrade r humble; to lower in rank, status, or esteem
 指使某人或某物在地位、声望或评价上下降，使其显得更低贱或更卑微。  

 The king ordered the general to abase himself before the nobles.  
 国王命令将军在贵族面前低头认错。  


## 2 abate 减轻  
Reduce, diminish
 使（程度、强度等）降低，减轻。  
 
 The storm eventually abated, and the sun came out.  
 风暴最终平息了，太阳出来了。  

## 3 abdicate
 放弃王位（或其他权力或责任）  
- Formally give up the throne (or some other power or responsibility)
  指正式地放弃统治权、权力或职责，通常用于君主或领导者主动让位的情况。
- 
- **English Example Sentence**: The king decided to abdicate in favor of his son.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 国王决定将王位让给他的儿子。  


4.  aberrant
Abnormal, deviant

> ## 1. aberrant
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈbɛrənt/
- **Chinese Translation**: 反常的
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指偏离正常或标准的行为、状态或特征，具有异常或不寻常的性质。
- **English Example Sentence**: His aberrant behavior made the other students very uncomfortable.
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的反常行为让其他同学感到非常不适。

### 3.1 Definition (Original)
Abnormal, deviant

5.  abeyance
Temporary suspension, inactivity

> ## 1. abeyance
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈbeɪəns/
- **Chinese Translation**: 暂停状态
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某事物暂时中止或停止活动的状态，通常是因为某种原因暂时无法进行。
- **English Example Sentence**: The company put its expansion plans in abeyance due to financial difficulties.
- **中文例句翻译**: 由于财务困难，该公司暂时搁置了扩张计划。

6.  abhor
Detest, regard with disgust

> ## 1. abhor  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈhɔːr/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 憎恶  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示极端的厌恶或憎恨，通常用于对某种行为、想法或事物的强烈反感。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She abhorred the idea of lying to her friends.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她憎恶对朋友撒谎的想法。  

### 3.2 Definition (Original)  
Detest, regard with disgust

7. abjure
Give up, renounce; repudiate, recant, or shun (especially formally or under oath)

> ## 1. abjure  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈdʒʊər/  
- **中文翻译**: 放弃、弃绝  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指正式或在誓言下放弃某种信念、权利或承诺，通常带有法律或宗教色彩。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The accused abjured his former beliefs under oath.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 被告在宣誓下弃绝了他以前的信仰。  

### 3.3 Definition (Original)  
Give up, renounce; repudiate, recant, or shun (especially formally or under oath)

8. abrasive
Rough, suitable for grinding or polishing (such as sandpaper); causing irritation or annoyance

> ## 1. abrasive  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈbreɪsɪv/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 磨蚀的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指粗糙的、适合研磨或抛光的（如砂纸）；或指引起刺激或烦恼的。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The abrasive nature of the sandpaper made it difficult to work with.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 砂纸粗糙的特性使得使用起来很困难。  

### 3.4 Definition (Original)  
Rough, suitable for grinding or polishing (such as sandpaper); causing irritation or annoyance

9. abreast
Side-by-side. The more common "abreast of" means keeping up with, staying aware of, or remaining equal in progress with.

> ## 1. abreast  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈbreɪst/  
- **中文翻译**: 并列的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指两个或多个事物并排、并列地存在或发生。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The two ships were sailing abreast of each other across the wide ocean.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 两艘船在广阔的海洋上并排航行。  

### 3.5 Definition (Original)  
Side-by-side. The more common "abreast of" means keeping up with, staying aware of, or remaining equal in progress with.

10. abridge
Reduce or lessen; shorten by omitting parts
throughout while retaining the main idea

> ## 1. abridge  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈbraɪdʒ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 概括  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 减少或降低；通过省略部分内容而使事物变短或简化，同时保留主要意思。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The teacher asked the students to abridge the story to make it easier to understand.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 老师让同学们概括这个故事，以便更容易理解。  

### 3.6 Definition (Original)  
Reduce or lessen; shorten by omitting parts  
throughout while retaining the main idea


11. abscission
Cutting off; sudden termination; the separation of leaves, petals, or other parts from a plant or animal

> ## 1. abscission  
- **Pronunciation**: /əbˈsiːʃn/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 脱落；突然终止  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指植物或动物的某部分（如叶子、花瓣等）脱落，或某事物突然终止。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The abscission of the leaf is a natural process in the life cycle of a plant.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 叶子的脱落是植物生命周期中的自然过程。

12. abscond
Depart suddenly and secretively

> ## 1. abscond  
- **Pronunciation**: /əbˈkɒnd/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 逃走  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某人突然且秘密地离开，通常带有非法或逃避责任的意味。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The thief absconded with the jewelry before the police arrived.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 小偷在警察到达之前带着珠宝逃走了。

13. abstain
Hold back, refrain (especially from something bad or unhealthy); decline to vote

> ## 1. abstain  
- **Pronunciation**: /əbˈsteɪn/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 拒绝（尤其指拒绝做坏事或不健康的事）；弃权  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示主动克制自己不做某事，尤其是避免不良或有害的行为，也可用于投票时选择不参与。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She decided to abstain from the discussion to avoid conflict.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她决定在讨论中保持中立，以避免冲突。

14. abyss
A deep and vast space or cavity; anything
profound or infinite

> ## 1. abyss  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈæbɪs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 深渊  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一个深邃而广阔的空间或空腔；也可用来形容极其深奥或无限的事物。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The ocean's depths are an abyss of mystery.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 海洋深处是一个充满谜团的深渊。


15. accede
Agree, give consent; assume power (usually as "accede to")

> ## 1. accede  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈsiːd/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 同意，表示同意；取得权力（通常用作“accede to”）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: “accede” 指同意某事或接受某项要求，也可指某人继位或取得权力。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The president acceded to the request for an investigation.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 总统同意了进行调查的请求。

16. accretion   Gradual increase; an added part or addition

> ## 1. accretion  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈkriːʃn/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 积累；逐渐增加  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指逐渐增加的过程或新增的部分，常用于描述自然或抽象事物的累积。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The accretion of knowledge over time leads to greater understanding.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 随着时间推移，知识的积累会导致更深入的理解。

17. acerbic
Sour; harsh or severe

> ## 1. acerbic  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈɛsər.bɪk/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 酸涩的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容味道酸涩的，也比喻言辞尖锐刻薄，态度冷淡。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Her acerbic remarks made everyone uncomfortable.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她尖锐的评论让每个人都不自在。

18. acidulous   Slightly acid or sour; sharp or caustic

> ## 1. acidulous  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈsɪdjuːləs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 酸涩的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容味道略微酸或涩，带有尖锐或刺激性。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The fruit has a slightly acidulous taste.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种水果的味道略带酸涩。

19. acme
Summit, peak, highest point

> ## 1. acme  
- **Pronunciation**: /æksiːm/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 顶点  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某个领域、活动或过程的最高点或巅峰状态。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The company reached its acme in 2020 with the launch of its groundbreaking product.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这家公司在2020年凭借其突破性产品达到了巅峰。

20. activism
The practice of pursuing political or other goals through vigorous action, often including protests and demonstrations

> ## activism  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈkɑːvɪzəm/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 激进主义  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过积极行动（如抗议和示威）来追求政治或其他目标的行为或实践。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The activist group organized a series of protests against the government's environmental policies.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这个激进组织组织了一系列抗议活动，反对政府的环保政策。

21. acumen
Keen, quick, accurate insight or judgment

> ## 1. acumen  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈkjuːmən/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 理解力  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指敏锐、迅速且准确的洞察力或判断力。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His business acumen helped him make profitable decisions quickly.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他敏锐的商业判断力使他能迅速做出有利可图的决策。

22. adhere
Stick (to), such as with glue, or to a plan or belief

> ## 1. adhere
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈdhaɪər/
- **Chinese Translation**: 遵守
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指按照计划、信念等坚持或遵循，也可指用胶水等粘附。
- **English Example Sentence**: The scientist adhered to his research plan despite the challenges.
- **中文例句翻译**: 面对挑战，这位科学家仍然坚持他的研究计划。

23. admonish
Mildly scold; caution, advise, or remind to do something

> ## 1. admonish  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈdɒmɪʃ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 警告  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用温和的责备或提醒的方式劝告某人，使其注意或改正行为。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The teacher admonished the student for talking during the lecture.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 老师提醒学生在上课时不要讲话。

24. adulterate
Make impure by adding inappropriate or inferior ingredients

> ## 1. adulterate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈdʒʌtəˌreɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 混杂  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过添加不适当或劣质成分使某物变得不纯。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The manufacturer was found guilty of adulterating the food with harmful chemicals.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 该制造商被发现向食品中添加有害化学物质。

25. adumbrate Give a rough outline of; foreshadow; reveal only partially; obscure

> ## 1. adumbrate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈdʌmbrət/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 概述；预示；部分显露；模糊  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示对某事物进行粗略的概述，或预示其未来的发展，也可能指只部分显露或使某事物变得模糊不清。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The first chapter adumbrates the themes that will be explored in the novel.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 第一章概述了小说中将探讨的主题。

26. adverse
Opposing, harmful

> ## 1. adverse  
- **Pronunciation**: /ədˈvɜːrs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 相反的，有害的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示与某事物相对立或产生负面影响的性质。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The adverse effects of the medication can be serious.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种药物的副作用可能很严重。



27. advocate
Speak or argue in favor of (verb); a person
who pleads for a cause or on behalf of another person (noun)

> ## 1. advocate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈdɒkvət/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 倡导者；支持  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为动词时，表示支持、提倡；作为名词时，指为某事或为他人辩护的人。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The lawyer is an advocate for the rights of children.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这位律师是儿童权利的倡导者。

28. aerie
Dwelling or fortress built on a high place; the
nest of a bird of prey, such as an eagle or hawk, built on a mountain or cliff

> ## 1. aerie  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈɛri/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 高处的居所或堡垒  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指建在高处的住所或堡垒，也指猛禽（如鹰或鹰隼）建在山崖或峭壁上的巢穴。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The eagle built its aerie high on the mountain cliff.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 鹰在山崖上筑起了它的巢穴。

29. aesthetic
Concerning the appreciation of beauty or good
taste, pertaining to the science of what is beautiful (adj); a sense of beauty and taste of a particular time and place (noun)

> ## 1. aesthetic  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈsthiːtɪk/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 审美（的）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为形容词时，指与美或良好品味的欣赏相关的；作为名词时，指某一特定时代或地方的审美和品味感。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The museum exhibits a wide range of aesthetic styles from different periods.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这个博物馆展示了不同时期的各种审美风格。

30. affable
Warm and friendly, pleasant, approachable

> ## 1. affable
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈfæbəl/
- **Chinese Translation**: 和蔼可亲的
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一个人态度友好、亲切，容易接近。
- **English Example Sentence**: Her affable nature made her a popular teacher among students.
- **中文例句翻译**: 她和蔼可亲的性格使她深受学生喜爱。

31. affectation
Fake behavior (such as in speech or dress)
adopted to give a certain impression

> ## 1. affectation  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈfɛkʃən/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 伪装行为  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指为了营造某种印象而刻意表现出的不自然的行为，如说话或着装方面的做作表现。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Her affected manner made it clear that she was trying to impress the interviewer.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她做作的举止清楚地表明她是在试图给面试官留下好印象。


32. aggrandize
Make greater; exaggerate

> ## 1. aggrandize  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈɡrændˌaɪz/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 加大；夸大  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过夸张或扩大来使某事物显得更加重要或显著。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The politician tried to aggrandize his achievements to gain more support.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这位政治家试图夸大自己的成就以获得更多支持。

33. aggregate
Gather together, amount to (verb);
constituting a whole made up of constituent parts (adj)

> ## 1. aggregate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈɡrɛdʒɪˌeɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 聚集；合计（动词）；由构成部分组成的整体（形容词）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为动词时，指把零散的东西聚集在一起或合计；作为形容词时，指由多个部分组成的整体。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The report aggregates data from multiple sources.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这份报告汇总了多个来源的数据。

34. alacrity
Cheerful or speedy willingness

> ## 1. alacrity  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈlækrəti/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 愉快或迅速的意愿  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示一个人乐于做某事，且行动迅速。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She responded with alacrity to the new assignment.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她愉快而迅速地接受了新任务。

35. albeit
Although, even though

> ## 1. albeit  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈlaɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 尽管  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示让步，相当于“虽然……但是……”，用于引出与前面所述情况相反或矛盾的信息。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Although it was a long journey, we decided to go anyway.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 虽然这是一段漫长的旅程，但我们还是决定去。

36. alienate
Cause to become unfriendly, hostile, or
distant

> ## 1. alienate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈliːənɪˌeɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 使疏远  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 使某人变得不友好、敌对或疏远。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His rude behavior alienated the customers.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他粗鲁的行为让顾客感到疏远。


37. alleviate
Lessen, make easier to endure

> ## 1. alleviate
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈliːviət/
- **Chinese Translation**: 缓解
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指减轻某种痛苦、困难或压力，使其更容易承受。
- **English Example Sentence**: The new medicine can alleviate the symptoms of the illness.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种新药可以缓解疾病的症状。

38. aloof
Distant physically or emotionally; reserved;
indifferent

> ## 1. aloof  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈluːf/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 冷淡的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指在情感或心理上保持距离，不亲近他人。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She kept an aloof attitude towards everyone at the party.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她在派对上对所有人都保持冷淡的态度。  

## 4 indifferent  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɪnˈdɪfərənt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 漠不关心的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指对某事不感兴趣、不关心或不偏不倚的态度。  
- **English Example Sentence**: He showed no interest in the outcome of the game; he was indifferent.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他对比赛的结果毫不关心。


39. amalgamate
Blend, merge, or unite

> ## 1. amalgamate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈmælɡəmeɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 合并  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 将两个或多个事物结合在一起，使其成为统一的整体。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The two companies decided to amalgamate their operations to increase efficiency.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这两家公司决定合并他们的业务以提高效率。

40. ambiguous
Not clear, hard to understand, open to having
several meanings or interpretations

> ## 1. ambiguous  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈmʌbɪɡ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 模棱两可的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 不明确的，难以理解的，可能有多种含义或解释。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The instructions were ambiguous, so it was unclear what to do.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 指示模棱两可，因此不清楚该做什么。


41. ambivalent
Uncertain; unable to decide, or wanting to do
two contradictory things at once

> ## 1. ambivalent  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈmɪbivəl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 模棱两可的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 对某事感到矛盾或不确定，同时想要做两件互相矛盾的事。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She felt ambivalent about the job offer because it meant moving away from her family.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她对这份工作机会感到模棱两可，因为这意味着要离开家人。


42. ameliorate
Improve; make better or more bearable

> ## 1. ameliorate  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈmiːliəreɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 改善  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 使变得更好或更容易忍受，通常指通过努力使情况有所好转。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The new policy is expected to ameliorate the working conditions for employees.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 新政策预计会改善员工的工作条件。

43. amortize
Gradually pay off a debt, or gradually write off
an asset

> ## 1. amortize  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈmɔːr.təɪz/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 摊销  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指逐渐偿还债务或逐渐冲销资产的价值。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The company plans to amortize the cost of the new equipment over the next five years.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 公司计划在未来五年内逐步摊销新设备的成本。  
---


44. anachronism
Something that is not in its correct historical
time; a mistake in chronology, such as by assigning a person or event to the wrong time period

> ## 1. anachronism  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈnækrənɪzəm/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 时代错置  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某事物不在其正确的历史时间中，或在时间顺序上出现错误，例如将某人或事件错误地归到错误的历史时期。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The play contains several anachronisms, such as a character using modern technology in the medieval setting.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这部戏剧包含多个时代错置的错误，例如一个角色在中世纪的背景下使用现代科技。

45. analgesia
Pain relief; inability to feel pain

> ## 1. analgesia
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈnɑːlˌdʒiːə/
- **Chinese Translation**: 镇痛
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过药物或其他方法减轻或消除疼痛的状态。
- **English Example Sentence**: The doctor prescribed a medication to provide analgesia for the patient's severe headache.
- **中文例句翻译**: 医生开了一种药物，以缓解患者严重的头痛。

46. analogous
Comparable, corresponding in some
particular way (making a good analogy)

> ## 1. analogous  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈnæləɡəs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 相似，可类比  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指两个事物在某些特定方面具有可比性，能够形成良好的类比关系。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The structure of the DNA molecule is analogous to a twisted ladder.  
- **中文例句翻译**: DNA分子的结构类似于一根扭曲的梯子。


47. anarchy
Absence of law or government; chaos,
disorder

> ## 1. anarchy
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈnɑːrki/
- **Chinese Translation**: 无政府状态
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指法律或政府的缺失，导致混乱和无序的状态。
- **English Example Sentence**: The country was plunged into anarchy after the war.
- **中文例句翻译**: 战争后，这个国家陷入了无政府状态。


48. annul
Make void or null, cancel, abolish (usually of

> ## 1. annul  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈnjuːl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 废除  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 使（法律或其他既定规则）失效或取消。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The court annulled the contract because it was signed under duress.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 法院裁定该合同因是在胁迫下签署的而予以废除。


49. anodyne

> ## 1. anodyne
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈnɒdɪn/
- **Chinese Translation**: 镇痛剂
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用于缓解疼痛的药物（名词）；缓解疼痛的（形容词）
- **English Example Sentence**: The doctor prescribed an anodyne to relieve the patient's severe headache.
- **中文例句翻译**: 医生开了一个镇痛剂来缓解患者的严重头痛。




50. anoint
Rub or sprinkle oil on; make sacred, such as by

> ## 1. anoint

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过仪式性地涂抹油来使某人神圣化，如加冕或任命宗教领袖。

- **中文例句翻译**: 国王在一场盛大的仪式中被加冕。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这个结果是一个异常现象；它不符合一般规律。

52. antagonize
Make hostile or unfriendly

> ## 1. antagonize  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈæntəˌnɑːz/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 激怒，挑衅  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 使某人感到敌意或不友好，通常指通过言语或行为激怒他人。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His rude comments were sure to antagonize the customers.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他粗鲁的评论肯定会激怒顾客。


53. antedate
Be older than, precede in time; assign to an
earlier date

> ## 1. antedate
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌæntɪˈdeɪt/
- **Chinese Translation**: 早于，早于某时间；将某事物归于更早的日期
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某事物在时间上早于另一事物，或被错误地归于更早的日期。
- **English Example Sentence**: The manuscript was antedated to make it appear older than it actually was.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这份手稿被提前标注日期，以使其看起来比实际更古老。


54. antithetical
Directly opposed, opposite; involving
antithesis (the rhetorical act of placing two phrases opposite one another for contrast, as in love me or hate me)

> ## 1. antithetical  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌæntɪˈθetɪkəl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 相对的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示直接对立、相反的，涉及对立的概念或事物。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The ideas of love and hate are antithetical.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 爱与恨是相对立的概念。  

## 5 antithesis  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌæntɪˈθɛsɪs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 对立  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指修辞手法中将两个相对的短语并置以形成对比，如“爱我或恨我”。  
- **English Example Sentence**: "Love me, hate me" is a classic example of antithesis.  
- **中文例句翻译**: “爱我或恨我”是对立修辞手法的经典例子。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这个失落之城的故事是不可靠的；至今没有确凿的证据支持它的存在。

- **English Example Sentence**: She was able to articulate her ideas clearly during the debate.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她在辩论中能够清晰地表达自己的观点。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容词指生活方式禁欲、简朴；名词指过着简朴、无物质享受生活的人，尤其是出于宗教原因的人。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这位僧侣的苦行生活体现了他深厚的宗教信仰。

88.  autonomous

- **Pronunciation**: /ˌɔːtəˈnɒməs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 自主的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某个实体（如系统、组织或个体）能够独立运作，无需外部干预或控制。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The car is designed to operate autonomously without human intervention.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这辆车设计为无需人工干预即可自主运行。

> ## 1. avarice  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈværɪs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 贪婪  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指无止境的贪婪，渴望占有财富，不愿分享。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His avarice led him to steal from his own family.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的贪婪使他偷窃自己家人的财物。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这位老师是学生创造力的催化剂。

(noun); to issue such disapproval or reprimand (verb)

> (noun); 表示不满或责备（verb）

136. chauvinism
Fanatical patriotism or blind enthusiasm
for military glory; undue or biased devotion to any group, cause, etc.

> ## chauvinism  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈʃoʊvɪnɪzəm/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 夸夸其谈  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指极端的爱国主义或盲目的对军事荣耀的狂热，也指对某一团体、事业等的过度或偏袒的忠诚。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His chauvinism towards his country led him to support the war without questioning its morality.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他对祖国的极端偏爱使他无条件支持战争，而没有质疑其道德性。

- **English Example Sentence**: The new policy was highly contentious among the employees.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这项新政策在员工中引发了极大的争议。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指能够阻止某人采取某种行动的事物，常用于描述威慑力或抑制效果。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The high cost of fuel is a deterrent to drivers buying new cars.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 高昂的燃油价格对司机购买新车起到了抑制作用。


223. diaphanous
Very sheer, fine, translucent

> ## 1. diaphanous  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌdaɪəˈfænəs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 透光的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指材质非常薄、细腻，光线可以透过，通常用于描述织物或材料。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The diaphanous fabric allowed light to pass through, creating a soft glow.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种透光的布料让光线透过，形成了柔和的光芒。

267. divine

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 通过占卜或超自然手段发现；凭借洞察力感知。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The oracle claimed to divine the future.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 那位神谕者声称能预知未来。

268. doctrinaire  Person who applies doctrine in an impractical
or rigid and close-minded way (noun); merely theoretical, impractical, or fanatical about other people accepting one's ideas (adj)

> ## 1. doctrinaire
- **Pronunciation**: /dəˈstrɪnəri/
- **Chinese Translation**: 教条主义者
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指那些不切实际、死板且固执地应用教条的人；形容对他人接受自己的观点过于理论化、不切实际或狂热的态度。
- **English Example Sentence**: He was a doctrinaire who believed that all political problems could be solved by following the party line.
- **中文例句翻译**: 他是一个教条主义者，认为所有政治问题都可以通过遵循党的路线来解决。

284. eclipse
The obscuring of one thing by another, such as the sun by the moon or a person by a more famous or talented person (noun); to obscure, darken, make less important (verb)

> ## eclipse  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɪˈkliːp/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 日食； eclipsing（动词）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一个事物被另一个事物遮蔽，例如太阳被月亮遮蔽，或一个人被更著名或更有才华的人遮蔽（名词）；也可指使某事物变得不显眼、不重要（动词）。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The new star eclipsed the previous one in popularity.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这颗新星在人气上超越了之前的那颗星。

substitute

> ## 1. ersatz  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈɜːrˌsɑːtʃ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 人造的，合成的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用来形容人工制造的、合成的物品，通常带有劣质或不正宗的意味。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The company produces ersatz coffee that lacks the rich flavor of real coffee.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这家公司生产的人造咖啡缺乏真正咖啡的浓郁风味。

318. erstwhile
Former, previous (adj); in the past, formerly
(adv)

> ## erstwhile  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈɜːrstwaɪl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 从前的，过去的（形容词）；曾经（副词）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用于描述过去存在的事物或状态，强调现在已改变。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The erstwhile leader of the company has retired.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 该公司从前的领导者已经退休了。

357. figurative
Metaphorical, based on figures of speech;
containing many figures of speech (as fancy- sounding writing); related to portraying human or animal figures

> **figurative**  
- **中文翻译**: 象征性的  
- **解释 (中文)**: 指使用比喻、隐喻等修辞手法的表达方式，而非字面意义。  
- **英语例句**: The poem uses figurative language to describe the beauty of nature.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这首诗使用象征性的语言来描绘自然的美。  

**containing many figures of speech**  
- **中文翻译**: 充满修辞手法的  
- **解释 (中文)**: 指文本中大量使用比喻、拟人、夸张等修辞手法，使语言更加生动形象。  
- **英语例句**: The essay is full of figures of speech, making it very engaging.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这篇文章充满修辞手法，使其非常引人入胜。  

**related to portraying human or animal figures**  
- **中文翻译**: 与描绘人物或动物形象有关的  
- **解释 (中文)**: 指与通过艺术手法表现人物或动物形象相关的创作或描述。  
- **英语例句**: The sculpture is related to portraying human figures in a realistic style.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这座雕塑与以写实风格描绘人物形象有关。

358. finesse
Extreme delicacy, subtlety, or diplomacy in
handling a sensitive situation or in a performance or skill (noun); use tact or diplomacy; employ a deceptive strategy (verb)

> ## 1. finesse  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈfɪn.sə/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 精湛技艺  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指在处理敏感情况或展示技能时表现出的极高细腻、微妙或外交技巧（名词）；用技巧或外交手段处理（动词）。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She used her finesse to navigate the difficult negotiation.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她运用精湛的技巧成功地应对了这场艰难的谈判。

359. flag

> flag  
- **Pronunciation**: /fæɡ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 精疲力竭，失去热情；垂下或下垂  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 该词表示因疲劳或失去热情而变得无力、下垂的状态。  
- **English Example Sentence**: After working for hours, he began to flag.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 工作数小时后，他开始感到精疲力竭。

A young bird that has just recently gotten its

> ## 1. fledgling  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈfledʒɪŋ/

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指刚长出羽毛的幼鸟，也可比喻为缺乏经验的新手，或形容新、不熟练的事物。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The fledgling company is still trying to find its place in the market.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这家初创公司仍在努力在市场中找到自己的位置。

- **中文例句翻译**: 他每天迟到，公然蔑视校规。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指偶然的幸运或意外的成功，而非通过努力或计划获得。

395. gouge
Scooping or digging tool, like a chisel, or a

> ## 1. gouge  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɡaʊdʒ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 挖凿工具；挖出；勒索  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为名词时，指一种用于凿刻的工具，如凿子；也可指用此类工具挖出的凹槽或孔洞。作为动词时，指挖出、剜出（如用拇指挖出眼睛），或勒索钱财。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The thief used a gouge to steal the jewels from the victim's eye.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 小偷用一种挖凿工具从受害者眼中偷走了珠宝。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一个逐步进行的过程，分阶段地发生。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The color change in the sunset shows a gradual gradation from orange to red.

397. graft
Insert part of a plant into another plant, where it continues to grow; join living tissue (such as skin) to part of the body where it will continue to live and grow; attach as if by grafting (verb); the part so grafted (as in a graft of skin); the act of acquiring money or other benefits through illegal means, esp. by abusing one's power (noun)

> ## 1. graft  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɡræft/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 嫁接  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指将植物的一部分插入另一株植物中，使其继续生长；或将活体组织（如皮肤）接到身体的一部分，使其继续存活和生长；比喻通过类似嫁接的方式附着；被嫁接的部分（如皮肤嫁接）；通过非法手段，尤其是滥用职权，获取金钱或其他利益的行为。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The surgeon performed a skin graft to replace the burned area.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 医生进行了皮肤移植手术，以替换烧伤的部位。

398. grandiloquent
Relating to lofty speech, esp. to the point of

> ## 1. grandiloquent  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌɡrændɪˈluːkənt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 华而不实的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指言辞华丽但空洞，带有浮夸、夸张或冗长的意味。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His grandiloquent speech made it clear that he was more interested in impressing people than in delivering useful information.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他那华而不实的演讲清楚地表明，他更在意的是给别人留下好印象，而不是传达有用的信息。

- **中文例句翻译**: 他在演讲中故意表现得夸张，让观众感到不舒服。

- **Pronunciation**: /ˈɡriːvəs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 令人悲痛的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 引起悲痛或痛苦的；非常严重、严重的。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The accident caused grievous injuries to several people.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这起事故导致了多人严重受伤。

- **Chinese Translation**: 镇定的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容一个人非常冷静，不会因为外界影响而感到不安或激动。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Despite the chaos around him, he remained imperturbable and focused on his task.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 尽管周围一片混乱，他依然保持镇定，专注于自己的任务。

449. impervious
Impenetrable, not able to be harmed or

> ## 1. impervious  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɪmˈpɜːrɪəs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 不可穿透的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容某物无法被穿透或无法被情感所影响，强调其不可渗透性。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The armor was impervious to bullets.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这件盔甲对子弹毫无防御作用。

- **English Example Sentence**: His impetuous decision to quit the job led to a period of financial instability.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他冲动地辞职，导致了一段经济不稳定时期。

- **Chinese Translation**: 暗示；含意

- **English Example Sentence**: The testimony has serious implications for the case.
- **中文例句翻译**: 该证词对案件有重大影响。

- **English Example Sentence**: The agreement was based on implicit understanding between the two parties.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这项协议是建立在双方之间的隐含理解之上的。

460. inasmuch
In like manner, considering that
(contraction of "in as much," generally followed by "as")

> ## inasmuch  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɪnˈæsmuːθ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 换句话说，考虑到  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示“考虑到”或“换言之”，用于引出对前文的进一步说明或推论。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Inasmuch as you are a student, you should attend classes regularly.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 换句话说，既然你是学生，就应该按时上课。

- **Chinese Translation**: 群岛的；孤立的；狭隘的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用来形容与外界隔绝、思想狭隘或局限于某一地区的人或观点。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His insular attitude made it difficult for him to work with people from different cultures.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他那种狭隘的态度使他难以与不同文化背景的人合作。

similarly established authority

> ## 1. insurrection  
- **Pronunciation**: /ɪnˈsʌrʃn/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 起义  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指针对政府或类似权威机构的武装反抗或叛乱行为。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The insurrection led to the downfall of the corrupt regime.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这场起义导致了腐败政权的崩溃。

498. interregnum
A time in between two reigns or regimes
during which there is no ruler; a period during which government does not function; any period of freedom from authority or break or interruption in a series

> ## interregnum  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌɪntəˈrɛɡnəm/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 间隙期  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指两个统治时期或政权之间的一段时期，期间没有君主或统治者，政府无法运作；也指一段摆脱权威或中断系列活动的时期。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The country experienced a long interregnum after the fall of the monarchy.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 国家在君主制崩溃后经历了一段漫长的间隙期。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这位病人的顽固性疾病需要新的治疗方法。

- **中文例句翻译**: 说话人的口音让大部分观众无法听懂他的讲话。

> ## 1. languid  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈlæŋɡwɪd/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 懒散的；迟钝的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容因疲惫而显得无精打采、迟钝的状态，缺乏活力。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The sun was languid, casting long shadows over the garden.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 阳光慵懒地洒落，为花园投下长长的影子。

> ## 1. leery

- **Chinese Translation**: 警惕的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 对某事持怀疑或戒备的态度，表示不信任或谨慎。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She gave me a leery look when I suggested the plan.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 当我提出这个计划时，她给了我一个警惕的眼神。

541. legerdemain

> ## 1. legerdemain  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈliːdʒədɛmən/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 麻将术语（指魔术师表演的魔术）；诡计或欺骗  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 该词原指魔术师的手法，现引申为欺诈或骗术，常用于描述以巧妙手段蒙骗他人的行为。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The magician used legerdemain to make the coin disappear.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 魔术师使用手法让硬币消失了。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容人懒散、嗜睡或反应迟钝的状态。

- **中文例句翻译**: 手术后的几天里，病人一直处于昏沉的状态。

- **中文例句翻译**: 他的话充满轻浮，使严肃的情况显得微不足道。

544. levy

> ## 1. levy  
- **Pronunciation**: /liːvi/

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为动词，指征收税款、对某国开战或征召人员入伍；作为名词，指征收税款的行为、应缴金额或征召入伍的行为。

- **中文例句翻译**: 政府决定对碳排放征收新税。

- **Chinese Translation**: 安抚
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指使愤怒的人平静下来或缓和其怒气。
- **English Example Sentence**: I tried to mollify my sister by offering her some chocolate.
- **中文例句翻译**: 我试着通过给她一些巧克力来安抚我的妹妹。


595. molt

> ## 1. molt
- **Pronunciation**: /mɒlt/
- **Chinese Translation**: 脱落
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指生物（如蛇）定期脱落皮肤、羽毛等的行为。

- **中文例句翻译**: 蛇会定期蜕皮以生长。

- **中文例句翻译**: 船长是个严守规章的人，坚持要求完美的秩序和守时。

closely; strict disciplinarian

- **English Example Sentence**: The book explores metaphysical questions about the nature of reality.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这本书探讨了关于现实本质的形而上学问题。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这份工作的单调让他感到无聊且效率低下。

598. moreover
Besides; in addition to what was just stated

> Moreover 是一个英语副词，意思是“此外”或“而且”，用于补充前面所说的内容。以下是其对应的中文翻译和解释：

**moreover**  
- **中文翻译**: 此外  
- **解释 (中文)**: 表示在之前所述内容之外，还有其他补充信息。  
- **英语例句**: Moreover, the project requires a lot of time and effort.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 此外，这个项目需要大量的时间和精力。

- **Pronunciation**: /əˈblaɪk/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 斜的；间接的；误导的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示倾斜的、斜的，也可指说话或行为间接、含糊其辞，甚至带有误导性。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His remarks were deliberately oblique, avoiding any direct answer.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的话故意含糊其辞，避而不答。


624. obsequious
Servile, very compliant, fawning

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容极度谄媚、讨好他人，表现出奴颜婢膝的态度。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His obsequious behavior made everyone uncomfortable.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他那种讨好的行为让所有人都感到不舒服。

- **中文例句翻译**: 新政策旨在消除手动输入数据的需要。


628. occlude

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指阻止液体、气体或光线通过，或使某物封闭、隔绝。

- **中文例句翻译**: 烟囱冒出的烟雾遮住了山的景色。

- **中文例句翻译**: 他那种多管闲事的评论让每个人都感到不舒服。

- **Chinese Translation**: 骨化  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指变得像骨头一样坚硬，或态度、观点等变得僵化、缺乏灵活性。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His ideas have ossified over the years.

643. ostensible or
Professed, evident, or pretended; outwardly
ostensive
appearing in a certain way

> ## ostensible or professed, evident, or pretended; outwardly  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈstenʃəl /  
- **Chinese Translation**: 显而易见的，声称的，假意的，表面的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 该词用来描述某事物表面上看起来是这样，但实际上可能并非如此。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His ostensible reason for leaving was to take a holiday, but in reality, he was escaping from his problems.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他声称离开的原因是去度假，但实际上是在逃避自己的问题。  

## 29 ostensive  
- **Pronunciation**: /əˈstenʃəs /  
- **Chinese Translation**: 表示的，指示的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 该词指通过某种方式表现出或显示出来的，通常用于指通过行为或语言表达的意思。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The ostensive meaning of the word is clear from the context.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这个词的表意从上下文中可以清楚地看出来。

663. pastiche
Mix of incongruous parts; artistic work
imitating the work of other artists, often satirically

> ## 1. pastiche  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈpæstɪʃ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 拼贴  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指将不协调或不相关的部分混合在一起，或模仿其他艺术家作品的艺术创作，常带有讽刺意味。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The movie is a pastiche of classic Hollywood films.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这部电影是对经典好莱坞电影的拼贴之作。

664. patent
Obvious, apparent, plain to see (adj); a letter
from a government guaranteeing an inventor the rights to his or her invention (noun)

> ## 1. patent  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈpeɪtənt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 明显的，明显的（形容词）；政府颁发给发明人的权利证书（名词）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为形容词时，表示“显而易见的”；作为名词时，指“专利”，即政府授予发明人对其发明的独占权利的证书。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The patent for the new drug was approved by the government last week.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种新药的专利上周得到了政府的批准。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某种物质或生物具有导致疾病的能力。
- **English Example Sentence**: The pathogenic bacteria can cause severe infections.
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种致病细菌会引起严重感染。


666. pathological Relating to or caused by disease; relating to compulsive bad behavior

> pathological  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌpæθəˈloʊdʒɪkəl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 病理学的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 与疾病有关的，或由疾病引起的；也指与强迫性不良行为有关的。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His pathological obsession with money led to his downfall.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他对金钱的病态痴迷导致了他的失败。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指数量极少的状态，通常用于描述资源、物品或某种现象的不足。

- **English Example Sentence**: He's such a pedant that he corrects everyone's grammar in the meeting.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他如此爱钻牛角尖，以至于在会议上会纠正每个人语法错误。

671. peddle
Travel around while selling; sell illegally; give

> ## 1. peddle
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈpɛdəl/
- **Chinese Translation**: 兜售
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指在旅行中售卖商品，或非法销售；也指散布、传播（如谣言、信息等）。
- **English Example Sentence**: The street vendor was peddling cheap knockoff watches.
- **中文例句翻译**: 那个街头小贩在兜售廉价的仿冒手表。


672. pedestrian
Ordinary, dull, commonplace

> ## 1. pedestrian  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈpɛdɪstrɪən/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 平淡的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指缺乏新意、普通、乏味的事物或行为。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His speech was so pedestrian that it bored the audience.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的演讲如此平淡，以至于让观众感到无聊。

Disparaging, derogatory, belittling (adj); a
name or word that is disparaging (noun)

> ## 1. pejorative  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌpiːdʒəˈrɑːtɪv/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 贬义的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容词，指带有贬低、侮辱意味的；名词，指具有贬低、侮辱性质的名称或词语。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The term "pejorative" itself is a pejorative term.  
- **中文例句翻译**: “pejorative”这个词本身就是一个贬义词。

- **中文例句翻译**: 那个解释非常透彻，即使是再复杂的概念也变得容易理解。

- **Pronunciation**: /ˈpenjəmbrə/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 本影区  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指日食或月食时，阴影的外层区域，也比喻任何事物周围模糊的边缘地带或存在不完全的区域。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The penumbra of the eclipse created a soft, dim light across the sky.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 日食的本影区让天空笼罩着一层柔和的暗光。

- **中文例句翻译**: 如果法律违反宪法原则，该法律本身即无效。

- **Chinese Translation**: 促使发生  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 使某事突然或过早地发生，通常指意外或迅速发生的情况。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The sudden loss of his job precipitated a series of events that changed his life forever.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他突然失业促使了一系列改变他一生的事件发生。


721. pr�cis
Concise summary, abstract

> **précis**  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈprɛsi/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 提要  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指对文章或作品进行简明扼要的总结，通常用于学术或商业文本。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The teacher asked the students to write a précis of the article.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 老师让学生写一篇这篇文章的提要。

- **Pronunciation**: /ˈkwerələs/

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指经常抱怨、不满或爱发牢骚的人。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Her querulous complaints about the weather made everyone uncomfortable.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她对天气的抱怨让每个人都感到不舒服。




768. quibble
Make trivial arguments or criticisms, find
faults in a petty way, esp. to evade something more important

> ## 1. quibble  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈkwɪb.əl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 争论琐事  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指对无关紧要的小事进行挑剔或争论，尤其用来逃避更重要的问题。  
- **English Example Sentence**: He spent hours quibbling about the exact wording of the contract.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他花了几小时争论合同中确切的措辞。

- **Pronunciation**: /kwiːˈɛsnt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 静止的，沉寂的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某物处于平静、无活动或无变化的状态。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The star was in a quiescent state for years before it exploded.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这颗恒星在爆发前数年一直处于静止状态。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: “repast” 作为名词时表示“餐食”或“宴会”，作为动词时表示“进食”或“大吃大喝”。

- **中文例句翻译**: 他们在皇家宴会中享用了丰盛的餐食。

- **中文例句翻译**: 这个剧院拥有丰富的经典剧目。

> ## 1. render

- **Chinese Translation**: 表达、提交、投降；翻译；正式声明；使成为  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: “Render” 有多种含义，包括“给出、提交、投降”等，也可以表示“翻译”或“正式声明”。此外，它还可以表示“使成为”某种状态。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The court ordered the company to render a detailed report by Friday.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 法院要求该公司于周五提交一份详细的报告。

808. retrospective  Looking to the past or backward; applying to

- **English Example Sentence**: The museum is hosting a retrospective of Picasso's work.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 博物馆正在举办一场毕加索作品的回顾展。

811. rhetoric
The art or study of persuasion through
speaking or writing; language that is elaborate or pretentious but actually empty, meaning little

> ## rhetoric
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈretərɪk/
- **Chinese Translation**: 修辞
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过言辞或写作来劝服的艺术或研究；也指那些辞藻华丽但空洞无物、实际上没有意义的语言。
- **English Example Sentence**: His speech was full of empty rhetoric and no real substance.
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的演讲充满了空洞的修辞，而没有实质内容。

- **English Example Sentence**: His ribald jokes made the audience uncomfortable.

813. ridden
Dominated or burdened by

> ## 1. ridden  
- **Pronunciation**: /rɪdən/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 被...支配或负担  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示某人被某种情绪、责任或压力所困扰或支配。  
- **English Example Sentence**: He was ridden by guilt after the accident.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 事故后，他一直被内疚感所困扰。

814. rife
Happening frequently, abundant, currently being reported

> rife  
- **Pronunciation**: /raɪf/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 普遍的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示某事物频繁发生或大量存在，常用于描述某种现象或情况。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The disease is rife in this region.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这种疾病在这一地区非常普遍。

815. rift
A gap or fissure (such as in rock), a break in friendly relations

> ## rift  
- **Pronunciation**: /rɪft/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 裂缝；分歧  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指岩石中的裂缝，或指友好关系中的破裂。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The earthquake caused a rift in the mountain.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 地震导致山体出现裂缝。

> ## 1. rococo  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈrɒkəkoʊ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 罗可可  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容装饰极其精致华丽（也可用于比喻，如在言语和写作中）；指18世纪法国盛行的一种高度装饰性的艺术和建筑风格。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The artist's work is characterized by a rococo style, with intricate patterns and delicate details.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这位艺术家的作品以罗可可风格为特点，具有精巧的图案和细腻的细节。

- **中文例句翻译**: 她眼中闪过一丝希望的光芒。

(adj); treat as though not very important; snub, ignore (verb); an act of treating in this way, a discourtesy (noun)

> (adj) 将某人视为不那么重要；轻视，忽视（动词）；以这种方式对待他人的行为，一种不礼貌的行为（名词）

897. supplant
Take the place of, displace, especially through
sneaky tactics

> ## 1. supplant  
- **Pronunciation**: /səˈplɑːnt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 取代  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过隐秘或不正当的手段将某人或某物挤掉，占据其位置。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The new company successfully supplant the old one in the market.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这家新公司成功地在市场中取代了老公司的地位。


898. supplicate
Pray humbly; ask, beg, or seek in a humble
way

> ## 1. supplicate  
- **Pronunciation**: /səˈplɪkət/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 乞求  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 以谦卑的方式恳求、哀求或寻求。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She supplicated the king for mercy.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她向国王恳求宽恕。


899. supposition
Assumption, hypothesis, something that has
been supposed

> ## supposition  
- **Pronunciation**: /səˈpɒzɪʃn/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 假设  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指在没有确凿证据的情况下所认为或接受为真实的情况、假设或假说。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His theory is based on a faulty supposition.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的理论是建立在一个错误的假设之上的。


900. surfeit
Excess, excessive amount, overindulgence

> ## 1. surfeit  
- **Pronunciation**: /sərˈfiːt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 过量；过多  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指超出正常或必要限度的数量或程度，常用于描述物质、情感或行为上的过度。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The surfeit of information can lead to confusion and decision fatigue.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 过多的信息会导致混淆和决策疲劳。

901. surly
Bad-tempered, hostile, unfriendly, or rude

> ## 1. surly  
- **Pronunciation**: /sɜːrli/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 性格暴躁的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一个人脾气不好，容易发怒，对他人的态度敌对、不友好或粗鲁。  
- **English Example Sentence**: He gave me a surly look when I asked for help.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 我请求帮助时，他给了我一个冷淡的眼神。

902. surmise
Guess, infer, think, or make an opinion with incomplete information

> ## 1. surmise  
- **Pronunciation**: /səˈmaɪz/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 推测  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用不完整的资料进行猜测或推断。  
- **English Example Sentence**: He surmised that the package might contain something valuable.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他推测这个包裹里可能装着有价值的东西。

903. surrogate
Substitute, person who acts for another
                  (noun); acting as a replacement (adj)

> ## 1. surrogate  
- **Pronunciation**: /səˈroʊɡət/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 代用品；代理人  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指代替某人或某物的人或事物，通常在原主体无法履行职责时发挥作用。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The mother chose a surrogate to carry her child.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这位母亲选择了一位代孕母亲来为她怀孕。


904. sybarite
Person devoted to pleasure and luxury

> ## 1. sybarite  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈsɪbəraɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 沉溺于享乐的人  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指极度追求享乐和奢华生活的人，常带有贬义。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The sybarite lived a life of constant indulgence in fine food and expensive clothes.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这个沉溺于享乐的人过着不断沉溺于美食和昂贵衣物的生活。

905. sycophant
Servile flatterer, parasitic person who fawns in order to get ahead

> ## 1. sycophant
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈsɪkəfənt/
- **Chinese Translation**: 奉承者
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指那种为了谋求私利而阿谀奉承、谄媚讨好的人。
- **English Example Sentence**: He is a sycophant who only cares about climbing the ladder, not about doing the job properly.
- **中文例句翻译**: 他是个只关心往上爬、而不关心做好工作的奉承者。

906. symbiosis
Mutually dependent relationship between two
organisms, people, groups, etc.

> ## 1. symbiosis
- **Pronunciation**: /sɪmˈbaɪəs/
- **Chinese Translation**: 共生
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指两个生物、人、群体等之间相互依赖、相互受益的关系。
- **English Example Sentence**: The relationship between the clownfish and the anemone is a classic example of symbiosis.
- **中文例句翻译**: 小丑鱼和海葵之间的关系是共生关系的典型例子。





907. synchronous
Happening at the same time; occurring at the

> ## 1. synchronous  
- **Pronunciation**: /səˈkroʊnəs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 同步的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指两个或多个事件在同一时间发生，或以相同速率重复发生。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The heart's contractions are synchronous with the electrical impulses in the heart.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 心脏的收缩与心脏内的电信号是同步的。

931. transitory
Temporary, short-lived, not lasting
932. synoptic
Relating to a synopsis or summary; giving a

## 34 synoptic

- **Chinese Translation**: 概括的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指能够简明扼要地总结或概述某事物的。

909. syntax
The rules governing grammar and how words
join to make sentences (or how words and symbols join in writing computer code), the study of these rules, or any system or orderly arrangement

放在一边稍后讨论，通常作为一种方式来

911. tacit
Understood without being said; implied, not stated directly; silent

> ## 1. tacit  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈtæsɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 隐含的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某种意思或协议未被明确说出，但被理解或默认。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The company's policy is tacitly agreed upon by all employees.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 公司的政策是所有员工默认同意的。

912. taciturn
Not talking much, reserved; silent, holding back in conversation

> ## 1. taciturn

- **Chinese Translation**: 沉默寡言的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一个人不善言辞，说话很少，性格内向，不轻易表达自己的想法。  
- **English Example Sentence**: He is a taciturn man who rarely speaks in meetings.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他是个沉默寡言的人，开会时很少说话。

918. terrestrial

Concise, brief and to the point (sometimes to the point of rudeness)

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示说话或写作简短、直截了当，有时甚至显得粗鲁。  
- **English Example Sentence**: Her reply was terse and to the point.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她的回覆简短而直截了当。

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一种充满愤怒和不满的激烈批评或攻击性言论，通常带有情绪化和侮辱性。

Someone who flatters or acts in a servile

- **English Example Sentence**: He was a loyal toady to his boss, always agreeing with everything he said.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他是个忠心的阿谀奉承者，总是附和老板说的话。


924. token
Sign, symbol, mark, badge; souvenir,
memento; coin-like disk used as currency for subways, arcade games, etc.; sample, or person, thing, idea taken to represent an entire group (noun); of very little or merely symbolic value (adj)

> token  
- **中文翻译**: 标志、符号、标记、徽章；纪念品；用于地铁、街机游戏等的硬币状货币；作为整体群体代表的样本、人、事物或观念（名词）；价值极低或仅具象征意义的（形容词）  
- **解释（中文）**: “token” 作为名词时，可以指代象征性的事物，如纪念品或代表整体的样本；作为形容词时，表示某物仅具象征意义或价值很低。  
- **英文例句**: The museum has a token of the ancient civilization.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 博物馆有一件古代文明的象征物。

925. tome
Large or scholarly book; one of the volumes in a set of several books

> ## tome

- **Chinese Translation**: 大部头书籍；多卷本中的一卷  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指一本厚重的、学术性的书籍，或一套多卷书籍中的一卷。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The ancient text was preserved in a leather-bound tome.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这部古籍被保存在一本皮革封皮的大部头书籍中。

- **English Example Sentence**: The company's innovation has fallen into a state of torpor.

927. torrid

> ## 1. torrid

- **Chinese Translation**: 炎热的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容非常热、干燥、灼热的天气，也可形容激情的、热烈的。

936. trite

- **English Example Sentence**: His speech was so trite that it failed to engage the audience.

939. turgid

- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指体积膨胀或过度膨胀的状态，也可比喻为浮夸、空洞的言论。

941. tyro

942. ubiquitous
Existing everywhere at the same time

> ## 1. ubiquitous  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌjuːbɪˈkwaɪt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 普遍存在的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某事物在各个地方同时存在，广泛分布。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The smartphone has become ubiquitous in modern society.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 智能手机在现代社会中已变得无处不在。

943. umbrage
Offense or annoyance (usually as take
umbrage, meaning become offended or annoyed)

> ## 1. umbrage  
- **Pronunciation**: /ʌmˈbrɑːdʒ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 感到冒犯  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 表示因某事而感到被冒犯或恼怒，通常指因他人言行而产生不满情绪。  
- **English Example Sentence**: I took umbrage at his comment about my work.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 我对他对我工作的评论感到不满。

944. unconscionable  Not guided by conscience; morally wrong,
unjust, unreasonable

> ## 1. unconscionable  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌʌnˈskɒnʃənəbl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 不合情理的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某事没有道德感，不公正，不合理，违背良心。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The company's actions were considered unconscionable by many employees.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 许多员工认为公司的行为是不可接受的。


945. undermine
Weaken, cause to collapse by digging
away at the foundation (of a building or an argument); injure or attack in a secretive or underhanded way

> ## 1. undermine
- **Pronunciation**: /ʌnˈdaɪm/
- **Chinese Translation**: 摧毁；暗中破坏
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过挖掘地基（如建筑物或论点）来削弱或导致崩溃，也指暗中或不正当的方式进行攻击或损害。
- **English Example Sentence**: His comments were intended to undermine the credibility of the entire project.
- **中文例句翻译**: 他的评论旨在破坏整个项目的可信度。

946. underscore
Emphasize (or, literally, to underline text)

> ## 1. underscore  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌʌnˈdərˌskɔːr/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 强调（字面意思为下划线）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 用于表示对某事物的重要性或关键性的突出强调。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The report underscores the importance of environmental protection.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这份报告强调了环境保护的重要性。

947. unearth
Dig up, uncover, expose

> ## 1. unearth  
- **Pronunciation**: /ʌnˈɜːrθ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 揭露，发现，挖掘  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指通过挖掘或调查，发现隐藏的事物或真相。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The archaeologists unearthed ancient artifacts from the site.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 考古学家从遗址中发掘出了古代文物。

948. unequivocal
Unambiguous, clear, absolute; having

> ## 1. unequivocal  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌjuːnɪˈvɔːkəl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 明确的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容毫无歧义、清晰明确，只有一种可能的含义。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The results of the experiment were unequivocal — the new drug was effective.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 实验的结果是明确的——这种新药有效。


949. unprecedented
Never before known or seen, without

> ## 1. unprecedented  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌʌnprɪˈzɛdənt/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 前所未有  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指从未发生过或从未被见过的，完全没有先例的。  
- **English Example Sentence**: This event is unprecedented in modern history.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 这一事件在现代历史上是前所未有的。


950. unseemly
Improper, inappropriate, against the rules

- **Chinese Translation**: 不合时宜的

- **English Example Sentence**: His unseemly behavior at the dinner party made everyone uncomfortable.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他在晚宴上的不合时宜的行为让所有人都感到不舒服。


951. unsparing
Generous, lavish (as in not sparing any

> ## 1. unsparing  
- **Pronunciation**: /ʌnˈspɑːrɪŋ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 慷慨的，毫不吝啬的（指不吝啬给予帮助或礼物给他人）；严厉的，毫不留情的（指不吝啬批评）  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 该词既可以形容慷慨大方，也可以形容严厉无情，具体含义取决于上下文。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His unsparing criticism of the project brought out the best in the team.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他对这个项目的严厉批评激发了团队的最佳表现。

952. untempered
Not toned down; not moderated,
controlled, or counterbalanced

> ## 1. untempered
- **Pronunciation**: /ʌnˈtemperd/
- **Chinese Translation**: 未经调和的
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指没有被克制、调节或平衡的状态，通常指情绪或行为未受控制。
- **English Example Sentence**: His untempered anger led to a violent outburst.
- **中文例句翻译**: 他无法控制的愤怒导致了一场激烈的爆发。


953. upbraid

- **Chinese Translation**: 责备  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 对某人进行严厉的批评或责骂，指出其错误。

- **中文例句翻译**: 老师严厉地责备那个学生又迟到了。





954. usury

> ## usury
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈjuːzəri/
- **Chinese Translation**: 高利贷
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指向贷款收取利息的行为，尤其是非法地收取极高或过高的利息。
- **English Example Sentence**: The bank was accused of usury for charging exorbitant interest rates on small loans.
- **中文例句翻译**: 银行因对小额贷款收取过高的利率而被指控从事高利贷行为。

993. yoke
A burden or something that oppresses; a frame
for attaching animals (such as oxen) to each other and to a plow or other equipment to be pulled, or a bar across a person's shoulders to help carry buckets of water, etc. (noun); to unite together or to burden (verb)

> ## yoke  
- **Pronunciation**: /joʊk/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 铐、负担  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 作为名词，指一种压迫性的负担，或用于连接牲畜（如牛）与犁具等拖拉设备的框架，也可指横跨肩部帮助搬运水桶等物品的横杆；作为动词，指将某物联结在一起或使某人负担重担。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The heavy yoke of oppression weighed heavily on the people.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 压迫的沉重枷锁使人民倍感负担。

994. zeal
Great fervor or enthusiasm for a cause, person,

- **Pronunciation**: /zil/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 热情  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 对某人或某事表现出极大的热忱或激情。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His zeal for learning made him stay up late every night.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他对学习的热情使他每晚都熬夜。

973. viscid or viscous

> 粘稠的

Thick, adhesive, or covered in something sticky

> 粘稠的、粘附的或覆盖着粘性物质的

etc.; tireless diligence in furthering that cause; passion, ardor

> 等等；不懈地致力于此事业的勤奋；热情，激情

974. vitriol
Something highly caustic, such as criticism
(literally, one of a number of chemicals including sulfuric acid)
975. vituperate
Verbally abuse, rebuke or criticize harshly
976. vociferous
Noisily crying out, as in protest
977. volatile
Varying, inconstant, fleeting; tending to violence, explosive
978. voluble
Easily fluent in regards to speech
979. wan
Unnaturally pale, or showing some other
indication of sickness, unhappiness, etc.; weak, lacking forcefulness

> ## 1. vitriol  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈvɪtrɪəl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 尖锐批评  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指极其尖锐、辛辣的批评，常带有侮辱性。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His vitriol towards the government was shocking.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他对政府的尖锐批评令人震惊。  

---

## 35 vituperate  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˌvɪtjʊˈpɛərət/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 激烈辱骂  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指用激烈言辞辱骂或严厉批评某人。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She vituperated her colleague for his incompetence.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她因同事的无能而对他进行了激烈辱骂。  

---

## 36 vociferous  
- **Pronunciation**: /vəˈkɪfərəs/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 喧闹的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容大声喧哗、抗议或表达强烈情绪。  
- **English Example Sentence**: The vociferous crowd demanded justice.  
- **中文例,句翻译**: 那群喧闹的群众要求正义。  

---

## 37 volatile  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈvɒlətaɪl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 易变的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容事物变化无常、不稳定，或容易激动、爆发。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His temper is very volatile.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他脾气非常易怒。  

---

## 38 voluble  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈvɒljʊbəl/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 善于表达的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容人说话流畅、健谈，能轻松表达想法。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She is a voluble speaker who never runs out of ideas.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她是个健谈的演讲者，从不缺乏话题。  

---

## 39 wan  
- **Pronunciation**: /wɒn/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 苍白的  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 形容脸色苍白或表现出虚弱、不悦等情绪。  
- **English Example Sentence**: His face was wan with exhaustion.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 他因疲惫而脸色苍白。


995. zenith
High point, culmination

> ## zenith  
- **Pronunciation**: /ˈziːnɪθ/  
- **Chinese Translation**: 顶点  
- **Explanation (Chinese)**: 指某个过程、发展或成就的最高点或顶峰。  
- **English Example Sentence**: She reached the zenith of her career when she won the Nobel Prize.  
- **中文例句翻译**: 她在获得诺贝尔奖时达到了事业的顶峰。
